id="d11517104e376-wk-Fact-CD89918B830C5CDA881175EC6E1EFEEE" name="dei:EntityEmergingGrowthCompany" contextRef="D2020Q3SD" format="ixt-sec:boolballotbox"><span Section 13(a) of the Exchange Act.  </span><span style="font-family:Wingdings;font-size:9pt;">o</span></div><div><br/></div><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><span style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br/></span></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"></hr><div><a id="s016489548DD054E686A6EE248F871F79"></a></div><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><span style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br/></span></div></div><div><br/></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;-sec-extract:summary;font-size:10pt;"><span style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">Item 5.02.  Departure of Directors or Certain Officers; Election of Directors; Appointment of Certain Officers; Compensatory Arrangements of Certain Officers.  </span></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:12px;text-align:left;text-indent:32px;font-size:10pt;"><span style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">Kathryn McLay, age 45, was appointed Executive Vice President, President and Chief Executive Officer of Walmart Inc.&#8217;s (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) Sam&#8217;s Club division, effective as of November 15, 2019.  In this position, Ms. McLay will report to the Company&#8217;s President and Chief Executive Officer.   Since February 2019, Ms. McLay has served as Executive Vice President, Walmart U.S. Neighborhood Markets.  Ms. McLay originally joined the Company in April 2015 as Vice President of U.S. Finance and Strategy.  She was promoted to Senior Vice President, U.S. Supply Chain in December 2015, in which role she served until February 2019.  Prior to joining the Company, Ms. McLay served for 14 years in a variety of strategic, finance, and supply chain roles at Woolworths Limited, a prominent Australian retailer, most recently as general manager for replenishment from October 2012 through March 2015. </span></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:12px;text-align:left;text-indent:32px;font-size:10pt;"><span style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">The Company has previously entered into a post-termination agreement and covenant not to compete with Ms. McLay dated December 24, 2015 (the &#8220;Non-Compete Agreement&#8221;).  The Non-Compete Agreement is substantially similar to the form of post termination agreement and covenant not to compete that is attached as Exhibit 10(g) to the Company&#8217;s Form 10-K filed on March 28, 2019.  The Non-Compete Agreement prohibits Ms. McLay, for a period of two years following termination of employment with the Company for any reason, from participating in a business that competes with the Company and from soliciting the Company&#8217;s associates for employment.  The Non-Compete Agreement also provides that, if Ms. McLay&#8217;s employment is terminated by the Company for any reason other than for a violation of the Company&#8217;s policies, the Company will continue to pay her base salary for two years following termination of employment.</span></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:12px;text-align:left;text-indent:32px;font-size:10pt;"><span style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">On November 14, 2019, the Compensation and Management Development Committee (the &#8220;CMDC&#8221;) of the Company&#8217;s Board of Directors approved changes to Ms. McLay&#8217;s compensation in connection with her new role effective as of November 15, 2019.  Specifically, Ms. McLay&#8217;s annual base salary will be $780,000.  Ms. McLay will continue to be eligible for an annual cash incentive under the Company&#8217;s Management Incentive Plan (the &#8220;MIP&#8221;), based on performance criteria established by the CMDC.  Ms. McLay&#8217;s annual target cash incentive payment under the MIP will be 180% of her base salary, with a maximum possible payout of 225% of her base salary.  Ms. McLay will be eligible to receive an annual equity award valued at $6,600,000, generally consisting of a combination of restricted stock and performance-based restricted stock units.  Ms. McLay will also receive an additional award of approximately 43,582 performance-based restricted stock units in connection with her promotion.</span></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:12px;text-align:left;text-indent:32px;font-size:10pt;"><span style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br/></span></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:8px;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><span style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">Item 9.01.</span><span style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;</span><span style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">Financial Statements and Exhibits</span></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:8px;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><span style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">None.</span></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><span style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br/></span></div><div><br/></div><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><span style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br/></span></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"></hr><div><a id="s12866E75CB275DA38749B00C903F7C79"></a></div><div><div
